糟了，是心动的感觉	Shit! [It’s] the feeling of falling in love. This expression is often used humorously to describe an unexpected attraction to someone or something.	魏无羡看到蓝忘机时，心里想：“糟了，是心动的感觉。”	When Wei Wuxian saw Lan Wangji, he thought to himself, "Oh no, it's the feeling of falling in love."	金凌第一次见到蓝曦臣时，心里想：“糟了，是心动的感觉。”	When Jin Ling first saw Lan Xichen, he thought to himself, "Oh no, it's the feeling of falling in love."	江澄看到蓝忘机时，心里想：“糟了，是心动的感觉。”	When Jiang Cheng saw Lan Wangji, he thought to himself, "Oh no, it's the feeling of falling in love."
你的良心不会痛吗	Doesn’t your conscience feel pain? This expression originated from an Internet joke about the bromance between Tang poets Du Fu and Li Bai. The joke claims that Du Fu wrote 12 poems for or about Li Bai, but Li Bai reciprocated with only one poem. The joke writer felt sorry for the “mistreated” Du Fu and questioned Li Bai if he felt guilty for his “cruelty” with the aforementioned expression. Regardless of its original interrogative tone, this expression is now often used humorously to tease someone.	魏无羡对蓝忘机说：“你的良心不会痛吗？你怎么可以这样对我？”	Wei Wuxian said to Lan Wangji, "Doesn’t your conscience feel pain? How can you treat me like this?"	蓝曦臣对金凌说：“你的良心不会痛吗？你怎么可以欺负小狗？”	Lan Xichen said to Jin Ling, "Doesn’t your conscience feel pain? How can you bully the puppy like this?"	江澄对魏无羡说：“你的良心不会痛吗？你怎么可以这样对待忘机？”	Jiang Cheng said to Wei Wuxian, "Doesn’t your conscience feel pain? How can you treat Wangji like this?"

鬼知道我经历了什么	<Expression> The ghost knows what I went through. God knows what I went through. This expression was first made popular by swimmer Fu Yuanhui during the 2016 Rio Olympics when she described her challenging training experiences. She used another Internet slang term 洪荒之力 [hóng huāng zhī lì] “preternatural power” in the interview. Her candid and humorous replies made her an Internet sensation.	魏无羡：鬼知道我经历了什么，但我从未后悔过。	Wei Wuxian: The ghost knows what I went through, but I have never regretted it.	蓝忘机：鬼知道我经历了什么，但这些都成就了现在的我。	Lan Wangji: God knows what I went through, but all of these experiences have shaped who I am today.	温情：鬼知道我经历了什么，但我选择微笑面对。	Wen Qing: The ghost knows what I went through, but I choose to face it with a smile.

歪个楼	<Expression> Slant the building. Let me digress. 樓 [lóu] as an Internet slang term refers to a post and its replies in online discussions. When you want to digress, you use this expression as a reminder to other Internet users.	魏无羡：歪个楼，我来说一个段子。	Wei Wuxian: Let me digress, I'll tell a joke.	江澄：歪个楼，我想聊一下最近的新闻。	Jiang Cheng: Let me digress, I want to talk about the recent news.	金凌：歪个楼，我有个有趣的话题要分享。	Jin Ling: Let me digress, I have an interesting topic to share.

A former Internet celebrity who is no longer popular.	蓝曦臣曾经是个过气网红，现在却是个知名导演。	Lan Xichen used to be a has-been internet celebrity, but now he is a well-known director.	金光瑶是一个过气网红，现在只能在小作坊里做美食视频。	Jin Guangyao is a former internet celebrity, now he can only make food videos in a small workshop.	温情曾是过气网红，如今却是一位成功的医生。	Wen Qing used to be a has-been internet celebrity, but now she is a successful doctor.

现充	adj./n. Reality+fulfilling. This Internet slang term comes from the Japanese Internet slang term “リア充” and refers to people who live a fulfilling life without ACG (Anime, Comic and Games) or the Internet.	金凌被称为现充，因为他的生活充实而没有沉迷于动漫和游戏。	Jin Ling is called a "现充" because his life is fulfilling without being obsessed with anime and games.	蓝曦臣不是现充，他整天都在忙于处理家族事务。	Lan Xichen is not a "现充" as he is busy dealing with family matters all day.	魏无羡虽然喜欢动漫和游戏，但也是一个现充，因为他的生活充实而有意义。	Although Wei Wuxian enjoys anime and games, he is also a "现充" because his life is fulfilling and meaningful.
还有这种操作	<Gaming terminology> Expression. This gambit exists?! An equivalent of “Didn’t see this coming.” This expression recently replaced 黑人問號 [hēi rén wèn hào] to express one’s confusion, amazement, or shock.	魏无羡看到蓝忘机突然变身，惊讶地说：“还有这种操作！”	Wei Wuxian was surprised to see Lan Wangji suddenly transform and exclaimed, "This gambit exists?!"	金光瑶看到魏无羡的巧计，惊讶地说：“还有这种操作！”	Jin Guangyao was amazed to see Wei Wuxian's clever tactics and said, "Didn’t see this coming!"	蓝曦臣看到云深不知处的美景，惊叹地说：“还有这种操作！”	Lan Xichen was amazed to see the beautiful scenery of Cloud Recesses and exclaimed, "This gambit exists?!"
我就笑笑不说话	<Expression> I’ll just smirk and say nothing. This expression is often used to show contempt.	江澄听到金光瑶的无理指责，只是冷笑一声，不说话。	Jiang Cheng just sneered and said nothing when he heard Jin Guangyao's unreasonable accusations.	魏无羡被冤枉时，只是笑笑不说话，心中却十分委屈。	When Wei Wuxian was wronged, he just smirked and said nothing, but he felt very wronged inside.	温情对待魏无羡，即使受到委屈，也只是笑笑不说话。	Wen Qing treats Wei Wuxian with warmth, even if she is wronged, she just smirks and says nothing.

Such novels are usually about wars and picking up women.	魏无羡喜欢看男频小说。	Wei Wuxian likes to read male-targeted internet novels.	蓝曦臣对男频小说不感兴趣。	Lan Xichen is not interested in male-targeted internet novels.	金凌写了一本男频小说，大受欢迎。	Jin Ling wrote a male-targeted internet novel, which was very popular.

This expression teases actress Zhou Dongyu’s relatively large distance between the eyes.	魏无羡学着周冬雨式凝视，逗得蓝忘机哈哈大笑。	Wei Wuxian imitated Zhou Dongyu's gaze, making Lan Wangji burst into laughter.	金光瑶的眼睛有点像周冬雨式凝视。	Jin Guangyao's eyes are somewhat like Zhou Dongyu's gaze.	蓝曦臣也会用周冬雨式凝视来逗笑弟弟。	Lan Xichen also uses Zhou Dongyu's gaze to make his younger brother laugh.
皮一下很开心	<Expression> [Of someone] deriving pleasure from being naughty. This expression is often used to comment on the intention of someone’s pranks or cheeky remarks.	魏无羡皮一下很开心，看到蓝忘机的表情。	Wei Wuxian is very happy to be naughty when he sees Lan Wangji's expression.	金凌皮一下很开心，捉弄蓝曦臣。	Jin Ling is very happy to be naughty and tease Lan Xichen.	温情皮一下很开心，逗笑了魏无羡。	Wen Qing is very happy to be naughty and made Wei Wuxian laugh.
抗日神剧	n. Epic dramas of the War of Resistance against Japan. This Internet slang term mocks TV dramas that blend history with fantasy to over-glorify the Chinese army in the War of Resistance against Japan. Such dramas are widely criticized by both the media and Internet users for distorting history.	魏无羡不喜欢看抗日神剧，觉得太不真实。	Wei Wuxian doesn't like to watch epic dramas of the War of Resistance against Japan, he thinks they are too unrealistic.	蓝忘机对抗日神剧的评价一直很严厉。	Lan Wangji has always been very critical of epic dramas of the War of Resistance against Japan.	温宁喜欢看抗日神剧，觉得很有意思。	Wen Ning likes to watch epic dramas of the War of Resistance against Japan, finding them very interesting.

地主家的傻儿子	n. The landlord’s silly son. This Internet slang term is often used affectionately to describe one’s adorkable male idol.	金凌虽然是地主家的傻儿子，但他有一颗善良的心。	Jin Ling, the landlord's silly son, has a kind heart.	魏无羡被粉丝称为地主家的傻儿子，因为他的搞怪可爱。	Wei Wuxian is affectionately called the landlord's silly son by fans because of his adorable antics.	蓝曦臣虽然是地主家的傻儿子，但他的聪明才智却无人能及。	Lan Xichen, the landlord's silly son, has unparalleled intelligence and wisdom.
明明可以靠脸吃饭, 偏偏要靠才华	<Expression> [Someone] could have clearly had meals with the face, but he/she chose to do so with talents and skills. “Have meals” means “make a living.” This expression means “[someone] could have made a living easily with his or her good appearance, but he/she insists on utilizing his or her talents and skills.” The expression is used to show recognition of someone’s becoming appearance and volition to learn skills and work hard.	魏无羡明明可以靠脸吃饭，偏偏要凭借自己的才华和努力。	Wei Wuxian could have easily relied on his good looks to make a living, but he chose to rely on his talents and hard work.	蓝忘机明明可以靠脸吃饭，但他更愿意用自己的才华赢得尊重。	Lan Wangji could have easily relied on his appearance to make a living, but he prefers to earn respect with his talents.	温情明明可以靠脸吃饭，却选择了靠自己的才华和勤奋工作。	Wen Qing could have easily relied on her looks to make a living, but she chose to rely on her talents and hard work.
社会主义巨婴	n. Socialist+gigantic+baby. The gigantic socialist baby. This Internet slang term pokes fun at Chinese adults who are not well-differentiated according the Murray Bowen’s Family Systems Theory. They often submit to authority figures. They are narcissistic, controlling, insecure, anxious, vulnerable, irritable, and depressed. It is possibly the Chinese equivalent of “Generation Snowflake.”	金光瑶被称为社会主义巨婴，因为她总是依赖他人而不愿意独立。	Jin Guangyao is called a gigantic socialist baby because she always relies on others and is unwilling to be independent.	温宁被称为社会主义巨婴，因为他总是依赖他人而不愿意独立。	Wen Ning is called a gigantic socialist baby because he always relies on others and is unwilling to be independent.	蓝曦臣被称为社会主义巨婴，因为他总是依赖他人而不愿意独立。	Lan Xichen is called a gigantic socialist baby because he always relies on others and is unwilling to be independent.
这盛世如你所愿	<Expression> This golden age, as you wished for. This expression is often used sarcastically to express discontent with government misconduct.	魏无羡对这盛世如你所愿的政府不满，他希望能改变现状。	Wei Wuxian is dissatisfied with the government of "this golden age, as you wished for," and hopes to change the status quo.	蓝忘机对这盛世如你所愿的社会感到失望，他希望能够改善人民的生活。	Lan Wangji is disappointed with the society of "this golden age, as you wished for," and hopes to improve people's lives.	江澄对这盛世如你所愿的现状感到愤怒，他决心要为民众谋取更好的生活。	Jiang Cheng is angry with the current situation of "this golden age, as you wished for," and is determined to seek a better life for the people.

口嫌体正直	/your lips say one thing, but your body language reveals what you really think (borrowed from Japanese)/	蓝忘机对魏无羡说：“你口嫌体正直，但我知道你心里在想什么。”	Lan Wangji said to Wei Wuxian, "Your lips say one thing, but I know what you're really thinking."	蓝曦臣口嫌体正直地说着感谢的话，但眼神却流露出无尽的愧疚。	Lan Xichen expressed his gratitude with his lips, but his eyes revealed endless guilt.	金凌口嫌体正直地说着不生气，但是手里的拳头却握得很紧。	Jin Ling said with his lips that he wasn't angry, but his clenched fists revealed otherwise.
NTR <Acronym>	This acronym is short for the Japanese phrase “Ne To Ra Re” (寝取られ). It means someone else slept with one’s date or partner.	魏无羡被人NTR了，心情十分复杂。	Wei Wuxian was NTR'd, feeling very complicated.	蓝忘机听说有人想NTR他的爱人，立刻变得愤怒。	Lan Wangji heard that someone wanted to NTR his lover and immediately became furious.	金凌发誓，绝不会让任何人NTR他的伴侣。	Jin Ling vowed never to let anyone NTR his partner.
麻辣鸡	n. Spicy+chick. This Internet slang term is a nickname for Nicki Minaj because it sounds like her last name “Minaj” and compliments her voluptuous figure.	金光瑶说她最喜欢的歌手是麻辣鸡。	Jin Guangyao said her favorite singer is "Spicy Chick" (Nicki Minaj).	金子轩在演唱会上大声喊着麻辣鸡的名字。	Jin Zixuan shouted the name of "Spicy Chick" (Nicki Minaj) loudly at the concert.	蓝曦臣收到了麻辣鸡的签名专辑，非常开心。	Lan Xichen received a signed album from "Spicy Chick" (Nicki Minaj) and was very happy.
课代表	n. Class representative. This Internet slang term refers to people who are good at explaining a hot topic for other Internet users. Internet users often call for a “class representative” humorously when they want to understand a complicated issue so that they don’t have to read about it on their own.	魏无羡在群里被称为课代表，因为他总是解释问题得很清楚。	Wei Wuxian is called the "class representative" in the group chat because he always explains things very clearly.	蓝忘机被朋友们戏称为课代表，因为他总是能够简单明了地解释复杂的问题。	Lan Wangji is jokingly called the "class representative" by his friends because he can always explain complicated issues clearly.	温情在网上被称为课代表，因为他总是能够用通俗易懂的语言解释复杂的话题。	Wen Qing is called the "class representative" online because she can always explain complicated topics in simple and understandable language.

叫兽	n. Roaring+beast. Depraved professors. This Internet slang term and 教授 [jiào shòu] “professors” are homophones. It is a cynical nickname for scholars who mislead the public with irresponsible comments or sexually harass the students. Their credibility is jeopardized by their own ignorance or depravity.	魏无羡发现一些叫兽教授在互联网上发表不负责任的言论。	Wei Wuxian discovered some depraved professors making irresponsible remarks on the internet.	蓝忘机对待学生非常严谨，绝不会成为叫兽教授。	Lan Wangji treats his students very seriously and would never become a depraved professor.	金光瑶被曝光性骚扰学生，成为了叫兽教授。	Jin Guangyao was exposed for sexually harassing students, becoming a depraved professor.
哏 (=梗)	n. Punch line, joke. This Internet slang term originally comes from Xiangsheng aka Crosstalk, a Chinese comedic performance, but it is made popular online through Taiwanese talk shows like Kangxi Lai Le aka Kangsi Coming. #Cai Kangyong and Little S Bid Farewell to Kangsi Coming# #蔡康永小S告别康熙#	魏无羡总是说一些哏，逗得蓝忘机哈哈大笑。	Wei Wuxian always comes up with punch lines, making Lan Wangji burst into laughter.	蓝曦臣的相声功底很深厚，讲的哏总是让人捧腹大笑。	Lan Xichen has a deep foundation in crosstalk, and his jokes always make people laugh heartily.	金凌学习相声，但是他的哏总是让人哭笑不得。	Jin Ling is learning crosstalk, but his punch lines always make people laugh and cry at the same time.
确认过眼神	<Expression> Confirmed the look in [his/her] eyes. I can tell from the look. This expression originally came from JJ Lin aka Lin Junjie’s song “Tales of the Red Cliff,” the theme song of the online game Red Cliff. Now it is used humorously to show one’s certainty about something.	蓝忘机确认过眼神，魏无羡肯定又在惹麻烦。	Lan Wangji confirmed the look in Wei Wuxian's eyes and was sure that he was causing trouble again.	魏无羡确认过眼神，觉得蓝忘机对自己的态度有所改变。	Wei Wuxian confirmed the look in Lan Wangji's eyes and felt that his attitude towards him had changed.	蓝曦臣确认过眼神，知道弟弟心里有话想说。	Lan Xichen confirmed the look in his brother's eyes and knew that he had something to say.
狗带	/(Internet slang) to go away/to slink off/(transliteration of "go die", possibly from 去死[qu4 si3])/	魏无羡看到蓝忘机过来，赶紧狗带了。	Wei Wuxian saw Lan Wangji coming over and quickly slinked off.	金光瑶做错事之后，只能选择狗带。	After Jin Guangyao did something wrong, he could only choose to go away.	江澄看到魏无羡，不想和他吵架，只好狗带。	Jiang Cheng saw Wei Wuxian and didn't want to argue with him, so he had to go away.

As an Internet slang term, it refers to the emotional reminiscing about the past.	魏无羡对过去的回忆杀总是让他陷入沉思。	Wei Wuxian's emotional reminiscing about the past always makes him lost in thought.	蓝忘机的回忆杀总是和他的家族有关。	Lan Wangji's emotional reminiscing about the past is always related to his family.	金凌的回忆杀总是和他父亲金子轩有关。	Jin Ling's emotional reminiscing about the past is always related to his father, Jin Zixuan.
伟光正	adj. Great, honorable, and correct. This Internet slang term is short for 偉大，光榮，正確 [wěi dà, guāng róng, zhèng què], often used sarcastically.	蓝曦臣对自己的伟光正感到自豪。	Lan Xichen is proud of his own greatness, honor, and correctness.	金光瑶总是自诩为伟光正，但实际上却是心机深重。	Jin Guangyao always boasts of being great, honorable, and correct, but in reality, she is very scheming.	蓝曦臣用伟光正的言行感染了身边的人。	Lan Xichen's words and deeds of greatness, honor, and correctness have influenced the people around him.
你国	n. Your country. China. This Internet slang term is often used negatively and satirically, implying one’s unwillingness to side with the government on an issue.	魏无羡对政府的做法感到不满，经常使用你国这个词来讽刺。	Wei Wuxian is dissatisfied with the government's actions and often uses the term "your country" to mock.	蓝忘机不喜欢政府的政策，因此经常使用你国这个词来表达不满。	Lan Wangji doesn't like the government's policies, so he often uses the term "your country" to express his dissatisfaction.	金凌对国家的一些决定感到不满，因此经常使用你国这个词来讽刺。	Jin Ling is dissatisfied with some of the country's decisions, so he often uses the term "your country" to mock.

暴露年龄	v. To give away one’s age. This Internet slang term is often used when mentioning something that happened a long time ago and pokes fun at the speaker’s age. It is often used in self-mockery.	魏无羡在谈论小时候的游戏时，不小心暴露了年龄。	Wei Wuxian accidentally gave away his age when talking about childhood games.	蓝忘机总是暴露年龄，让人觉得他是个老灵魂。	Lan Wangji always gives away his age, making people feel that he has an old soul.	金凌在网上发了一张小时候的照片，被朋友们取笑暴露了年龄。	Jin Ling posted a childhood photo online and was teased for giving away his age.
带节奏	v. Lead+rhythm. <Gaming terminology> To instigate a fight. This Internet slang term is originally used to describe a gamer who determines the strategies for the whole team in a group video or computer game. Now it is used to describe an Internet user who misleads others with wrong information or offensive language in online discussions and instigates verbal fights among groups holding opposing views.	金光瑶在网上发表言论，意图带节奏。	Jin Guangyao made remarks online with the intention of instigating a fight.	江澄被人带节奏，险些陷入口水战。	Jiang Cheng was misled by someone and almost got into a verbal fight.	蓝曦臣看到有人在带节奏，立刻制止了争吵。	Lan Xichen immediately stopped the argument when he saw someone trying to instigate a fight.
一步两步， 是魔鬼的步伐	<Expression> One step, two steps, [it] is the gate of a devil. This expression comes from the widely ridiculed 2014 song “My Skating Shoes” by Pang Mailang. It is often used to describe clumsy and uncoordinated walking or dancing steps.	魏无羡跳舞时，一步两步，简直是魔鬼的步伐。	When Wei Wuxian dances, one step, two steps, it's truly the gate of a devil.	温宁学跳舞，一步两步，像是魔鬼的步伐。	Wen Ning tries to dance, one step, two steps, it's like the gate of a devil.	金凌走路一步两步，简直是魔鬼的步伐。	Jin Ling walks one step, two steps, it's truly the gate of a devil.
做一个精致的猪猪女孩	<Expression> Be a refined piggy girl. This expression scoffs at fangirls who like staying in and binge-watching videos featuring their idols. “Piggy” refers to their physical appearance and lifestyle. Due to the sedentary lifestyle, they are often believed to be overweight. The stereotype is undoubtedly pejorative and hurtful.	蓝忘机嘲笑江澄，说他女朋友是个精致的猪猪女孩。	Lan Wangji mocked Jiang Cheng, saying his girlfriend is a refined piggy girl.	魏无羡不喜欢被称为精致的猪猪女孩，觉得这个词很伤人。	Wei Wuxian doesn't like being called a refined piggy girl, he finds the term very hurtful.	温情和温宁一起看电视剧，被朋友们取笑是一对精致的猪猪姐妹。	Wen Qing and Wen Ning watch TV dramas together and are teased by their friends as a pair of refined piggy sisters.
上头姐妹	n. Intoxicated sisters.	蓝曦臣和蓝忘机喝醉了，成了一对上头姐妹。	Lan Xichen and Lan Wangji got drunk and became a pair of intoxicated sisters.	温情和江澄一起喝酒，变成了上头姐妹。	Wen Qing and Jiang Cheng drank together and turned into intoxicated sisters.	金凌和蓝曦臣在宴会上喝多了，成了一对上头姐妹。	Jin Ling and Lan Xichen drank too much at the banquet and became a pair of intoxicated sisters.

众人皆醉我独醒	<Expression> Everyone is drunk and only I am sober. This expression is quoted from a poem by Li Bai from the Tang dynasty, but now it is often used to describe a self-important person sarcastically.	蓝忘机对待琴棋书画，众人皆醉我独醒。	Lan Wangji treats music, chess, calligraphy, and painting with indifference, as if everyone else is drunk and only he is sober.	魏无羡总是自以为是，众人皆醉我独醒。	Wei Wuxian always thinks highly of himself, as if everyone else is drunk and only he is sober.	金凌对待叔叔的教诲，众人皆醉我独醒。	Jin Ling treats his uncle's teachings with indifference, as if everyone else is drunk and only he is sober.
什么仇什么怨	<Expression> What grudge do you hold against me? This expression first became popular in 2014 as a passenger’s reply to another passenger who tried to stop him from cracking melon seeds on the bus. They kept arguing for seven minutes while the melon seed cracker grumbled “What grudge do you hold against me [so that you keep pestering me]?” several times during the process. Now the expression is used as a comment on or complaint about an interpersonal conflict that one does not fully understand.	魏无羡对江澄说：“什么仇什么怨，我们兄弟之间不要计较。”	Wei Wuxian said to Jiang Cheng, "What grudge do you hold against me? Let's not dwell on the past between us brothers."	蓝忘机对魏无羡说：“什么仇什么怨，我只希望你能明白我的苦衷。”	Lan Wangji said to Wei Wuxian, "What grudge do you hold against me? I just hope you can understand my difficulties."	温情对温宁说：“什么仇什么怨，你要相信哥哥我是为了你好。”	Wen Qing said to Wen Ning, "What grudge do you hold against me? You have to believe that I am doing this for your own good."
诺兰黑	n./adj. Nolan+black. Christopher Nolan detractors. This Internet slang term is used to describe people who dislike Christopher Nolan’s film style.	魏无羡是诺兰黑，他不喜欢克里斯托弗·诺兰的电影。	Wei Wuxian is a Nolan detractor; he doesn't like Christopher Nolan's movies.	蓝忘机不是诺兰黑，他欣赏克里斯托弗·诺兰的电影风格。	Lan Wangji is not a Nolan detractor; he appreciates Christopher Nolan's film style.	金凌是诺兰黑，他对克里斯托弗·诺兰的电影评价不高。	Jin Ling is a Nolan detractor; he doesn't have a high opinion of Christopher Nolan's movies.
地图炮	n. map+cannon. Discrimination against people from a certain region.	蓝曦臣讨厌地图炮，他认为地域歧视是不应该存在的。	Lan Xichen detests discrimination against people from a certain region; he believes regional discrimination should not exist.	温情反对地图炮，她主张人们应该平等对待来自不同地方的人。	Wen Qing opposes discrimination against people from a certain region; she advocates for equal treatment of people from different places.	蓝湛对待地图炮持反对态度，他认为地域歧视是不公平的。	Lan Zhan opposes discrimination against people from a certain region; he believes regional discrimination is unfair.
外貌协会	/the "good-looks club": people who attach great importance to a person's appearance (pun on 外貿協會|外贸协会 foreign trade association)/	魏无羡不属于外貌协会，他更看重一个人的内在。	Wei Wuxian is not a member of the "good-looks club"; he values a person's inner qualities more.	蓝忘机反对外貌协会，他认为外表并不代表一个人的全部。	Lan Wangji opposes the "good-looks club"; he believes appearance does not represent everything about a person.	金凌是外貌协会的一员，他觉得外表很重要。	Jin Ling is a member of the "good-looks club"; he thinks appearance is very important.

low	adj. Showing poor quality or taste or moral standards. Usually written with the lowercase “l”, this word means tacky, tasteless, or immoral.	温宁觉得温青的行为很low。	Wen Ning thinks Wen Qing's behavior is tacky.	金光瑶的手段太low了，连自己的兄弟都害死了。	Jin Guangyao's methods are too immoral; he even caused the death of his own brother.	魏无羡不屑于和低劣的人斗嘴。	Wei Wuxian disdains arguing with people of low quality.
你还记得大明湖畔的。。。吗	<Expression> Do you still remember…by the Daming Lake? This question was originally a line from the 1998 TV show Princess Return Pearl [or My Fair Princess]. Ziwei confronted her birth father Emperor Qianlong, “Do you still remember Xia Yuhe by the Daming Lake?” Xia Yuhe is Ziwei’s mother and Ziwei was born out of wedlock. Now this line is used humorously to remind the listener or reader of something or someone.	魏无羡对蓝忘机说：“你还记得大明湖畔的那个夜晚吗？”	Wei Wuxian said to Lan Wangji, "Do you still remember that night by the Daming Lake?"	温情对温宁说：“你还记得大明湖畔的竹林吗？”	Wen Qing said to Wen Ning, "Do you still remember the bamboo forest by the Daming Lake?"	蓝曦臣问蓝忘机：“你还记得大明湖畔的那个人吗？”	Lan Xichen asked Lan Wangji, "Do you still remember that person by the Daming Lake?"

粗线	v. Bold+line. To appear, to show up. This Internet slang term and 出現 [chū xiàn] “come up, show up” are homophones. This term is a humorous way of saying “to appear” with a Taiwanese Mandarin accent.	魏无羡粗线了，大摇大摆地走了进来。	Wei Wuxian showed up, swaggering in.	蓝忘机粗线了，站在门口。	Lan Wangji appeared, standing at the door.	江澄粗线了，突然出现在人群中。	Jiang Cheng showed up suddenly in the crowd.
雾草	n. Fog+glass. This Internet slang term is a euphemism for 我操 [wǒ cào] “I fuck” because of the similar pronunciation.	魏无羡看到了一只雾草，不禁惊呼一声。	Wei Wuxian saw a foggy glass and couldn't help but exclaim.	蓝忘机踩到了一块雾草，差点摔倒。	Lan Wangji stepped on a foggy glass and almost fell.	江澄踢开了一块雾草，露出了下面的东西。	Jiang Cheng kicked away a foggy glass, revealing what was underneath.

This Internet slang term describes one’s shock at something that rendered himself or herself unsteady.	魏无羡看到蓝忘机的笑容，差点扶墙。	Wei Wuxian almost leaned on the wall when he saw Lan Wangji's smile.	蓝曦臣听到了一个笑话，差点扶墙。	Lan Xichen heard a joke and almost leaned on the wall.	温情看到了一幕令人震惊的场面，差点扶墙。	Wen Qing saw a shocking scene and almost leaned on the wall.
灵魂舞者	n. Soul+dancer. Soul dancer. This Internet slang term describes a person who botches a dance but exudes boundless confidence.	魏无羡跳舞时像个灵魂舞者，虽然舞步不准却充满自信。	Wei Wuxian dances like a soul dancer, full of confidence even though his steps are not accurate.	金凌虽然跳舞跌了好几次，但他是个灵魂舞者，毫不在意。	Jin Ling fell several times while dancing, but he is a soul dancer, completely unconcerned.	蓝曦臣跳舞时像个灵魂舞者，尽管舞姿欠佳，但表现得毫不在意。	Lan Xichen dances like a soul dancer, despite the lackluster performance, he acts as if he doesn't care at all.

不作死就不会死 (No Zuo No Die)	<Expression> If you don’t seek death, you won’t die. If you don’t do stupid things, you won’t suffer. This phrase is often used to comment on crazy behaviors that lead to embarrassment and awkwardness.	魏无羡总是不作死就不会死，他总是能化险为夷。	Wei Wuxian never seeks death, so he won't die. He always manages to turn danger into safety.	蓝忘机对待事情总是谨慎小心，所以他不会不作死就不会死。	Lan Wangji always handles things with caution, so he won't do stupid things and suffer.	金凌不作死就不会死，他总是很理智地处理问题。	Jin Ling won't suffer if he doesn't do stupid things; he always handles things rationally.
传送门	n. Convey+door. Door-shaped teleporter.【Computing】Portal, the link to a website. This Internet slang term often precedes a website link. It is also often used to request the link to more information on a subject.	魏无羡发了一条传送门，邀请大家一起观看莫玄羽的最新演出。	Wei Wuxian posted a portal, inviting everyone to watch Mo Xuanyu's latest performance.	蓝曦臣在微博上分享了一条传送门，指向他最新发布的音乐作品。	Lan Xichen shared a portal on Weibo, linking to his latest music release.	金凌在群里发了一个传送门，希望大家能帮忙转发。	Jin Ling posted a portal in the group, hoping everyone could help to repost.
饭拍	adj. Fan-shot. (Of videos) shot by fans.	蓝忘机的饭拍视频在网上引起了轰动，粉丝们都很喜欢。	Lan Wangji's fan-shot video caused a sensation online, and fans loved it.	魏无羡很喜欢看粉丝饭拍的视频，觉得很有趣。	Wei Wuxian enjoys watching fan-shot videos, finding them very interesting.	金凌的饭拍照片被粉丝们纷纷转发，赞美他的颜值。	Jin Ling's fan-shot photos were widely reposted by fans, praising his good looks.
付兰兰 / 腐兰兰	n. Fu Lanlan or Rotten Lanlan.. This Internet slang term is an affectionate nickname for James Franco because it sounds like his last name. “Lanlan” is traditionally a female name and 腐 [fǔ] as an Internet slang term means “obsessed with bromance or romance between two young men .”	魏无羡被粉丝戏称为“腐无羡”，因为他喜欢写男男情情。	Wei Wuxian is jokingly called "Fu Wuxian" by fans because he likes to write about romantic relationships between men.	蓝曦臣在网上被粉丝戏称为“腐曦臣”，因为他喜欢收集男男情情的书籍。	Lan Xichen is jokingly called "Fu Xichen" by fans online because he likes to collect books about romantic relationships between men.	金凌被粉丝戏称为“腐凌”，因为他喜欢看男男情情的动漫。	Jin Ling is jokingly called "Fu Ling" by fans because he likes to watch anime about romantic relationships between men.
砸简历	Smash+resumes. Expression. Smash [us with your] resumes. 厉害了我的哥	<Expression> Wow you rock, my brother. This Internet slang term came into popularity as a high school student’s comment on the dazzling gaming skills of his military training instructor who caught him playing The King’s Glory on the phone. Instead of confiscating the phone, the instructor unleashed his inner gamer and helped the student win the game. This expression is now used to express astonishment or amazement. The word “brother” is replaced in other contexts to address different people.	魏无羡厉害了我的哥，居然在不到一天的时间内解决了这个难题。	Wow, Wei Wuxian, you're amazing, my brother, you actually solved this problem in less than a day.	蓝忘机厉害了我的哥，他的琴艺真是没得说。	Wow, Lan Wangji, you rock, my brother, your musical skills are truly remarkable.	温情厉害了我的姐，她的医术让人叹为观止。	Wow, Wen Qing, you're amazing, my sister, your medical skills are truly breathtaking.

His supernatural power is time manipulation. 废柴	/(Cantonese) (coll.) good-for-nothing/loser/	温宁虽然看起来像个废柴，但实际上非常勇敢。	Although Wen Ning looks like a good-for-nothing, he is actually very brave.	魏无羡常常调侃江澄是个废柴，但心里却十分依赖他。	Wei Wuxian often teases Jiang Cheng as a loser, but deep down, he relies on him a lot.	金凌不愿意承认自己是个废柴，一直在努力证明自己。	Jin Ling refuses to admit that he is a good-for-nothing and has been working hard to prove himself.
带感	adj. carry+feeling. This Internet slang term is used to describe people or things that touch your heart, pique your interest, and/or bring you joy.	蓝曦臣的音乐总是很带感，让人听了很舒服。	Lan Xichen's music always carries a lot of feeling, making people feel very comfortable when listening to it.	魏无羡对蓝忘机的琴音十分带感，总是能引起他的共鸣。	Wei Wuxian is very touched by Lan Wangji's music and it always resonates with him.	温情的微博内容总是带感，让人感到温暖和快乐。	Wen Qing's Weibo posts are always very touching, making people feel warm and happy.
买买买	v. Buy buy buy! This Internet slang term is often used humorously to convey or provoke a strong desire to splurge.	金凌看到了新款游戏机，忍不住想要买买买。	Jin Ling saw the new game console and couldn't help but want to splurge.	魏无羡和江澄逛街时，总是兴奋地喊着买买买。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng always excitedly shout "buy buy buy" when shopping.	蓝忘机虽然不喜欢购物，但看到了心仪已久的书籍，也忍不住想要买买买。	Lan Wangji doesn't like shopping, but when he saw the book he had been longing for, he couldn't help but want to splurge.

QAQ	Emoticon. The emoticon looks like a sad face with a gaping mouth and a pair of teary eyes. It is often used to express sadness.	魏无羡看到蓝忘机受伤的样子，心里不禁涌起了一股悲伤，只能用QAQ来表达。	Wei Wuxian felt a surge of sadness when he saw Lan Wangji injured, and could only express it with QAQ.	金凌看到舅舅被欺负，眼中闪过一丝悲伤，心想：QAQ，舅舅要保护好自己。	Jin Ling felt a hint of sadness when he saw his uncle being bullied, thinking to himself: QAQ, Uncle, please take care of yourself.
你这是在搞事情	Expression. You are causing trouble for me. Actor Chen He frequently used this expression on the Chinese version of Running Man. Now this expression is used to vent or joke about unexpected or undesirable situations.	蓝忘机对魏无羡说：“你这是在搞事情，又惹出什么麻烦了？”	Lan Wangji said to Wei Wuxian, "You are causing trouble for me again, what kind of trouble have you stirred up this time?"	金光瑶看到魏无羡和蓝忘机在一起，不禁嘀咕：“你这是在搞事情，这可怎么办？”	Jin Guangyao saw Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji together, couldn't help but mutter, "You are causing trouble for me, what should I do about this?"
E神	n. E+deity. A nickname for Eason Chan, a Hong Kong singer, because it sounds like “Eason.”	金子轩是E神的粉丝，经常听他的歌。	Jin Zixuan is a fan of Eason Chan and often listens to his songs.	蓝曦臣在演唱会上见到了E神，激动地合影留念。	Lan Xichen met Eason Chan at the concert and excitedly took a photo with him.	魏无羡和江澄商量着要去E神的演唱会，准备好好享受一番。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng discussed going to Eason Chan's concert, preparing to enjoy themselves.
萌萌哒	/(Internet slang) adorable/cute/	金凌小时候的照片实在是太萌萌哒了，简直让人忍不住想捏一把。	Jin Ling's childhood photos are so adorable, it's almost irresistible to pinch his cheeks.	蓝忘机看到魏无羡的模样，忍不住感叹：“你这是萌萌哒的模样吗？”	Lan Wangji couldn't help but exclaim when he saw Wei Wuxian's appearance, "Is this your adorable look?"	温情和温情的宠物一起玩耍，场面实在是太萌萌哒了。	Wen Qing and her pet playing together is really adorable. 
毁童年	adj. Destroy+childhood. (Of things) leading to the disillusionment about childhood. This Internet slang term is often used to describe a parody of childhood idols or favorites.	金光瑶看到魏无羡和蓝忘机的对决，心想：“这简直是要毁童年啊！”	Jin Guangyao saw the confrontation between Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji, thinking to himself, "This is simply going to ruin my childhood!"	金子轩看到自己小时候的玩具被弄坏了，心里不禁感叹：“这简直是要毁童年啊！”	Jin Zixuan saw his childhood toys being broken, couldn't help but sigh, "This is simply going to ruin my childhood!"	蓝曦臣看到了一部关于童年回忆的恶搞视频，觉得这简直是要毁童年。	Lan Xichen saw a parody video about childhood memories and felt that it was simply going to ruin his childhood.

A站	A site aka Acfun. B站 [B zhàn] B site aka bilibili. Both are interactive video sharing websites themed around anime, manga, game, movie, music, and TV fandom based in China. They also both feature “barrage,” a real-time on-screen user commentary system.	魏无羡喜欢在A站上观看动漫。	Wei Wuxian likes to watch anime on A site.	金凌在B站上发布了他的音乐作品。	Jin Ling posted his music works on B site.	蓝曦臣在A站和B站上都有很多粉丝。	Lan Xichen has many fans on both A site and B site.
湾湾	n. Wan Wan. This Internet slang term was created by Mainland Internet users as a nickname for Taiwan or the Taiwanese people.	魏无羡计划去湾湾旅行。	Wei Wuxian plans to travel to Taiwan.	金凌的舅舅是湾湾人。	Jin Ling's uncle is from Taiwan.	蓝曦臣很喜欢湾湾的美食。	Lan Xichen really likes Taiwanese cuisine.
塘主	n. [Fish] pond owner. This Internet slang term is a pejorative nickname for Zhang Han, because his famous line in the TV show Boss & Me:  “I want to let everyone know: This fish pond, is now under your management by contract.” People jeer his role for making a ludicrous confession of love by mentioning a fish pond. The nickname implies discrimination against country people and contempt for Zhang Han.	魏无羡觉得塘主这个绰号很有趣。	Wei Wuxian finds the nickname "pond owner" very interesting.	金凌不喜欢别人用塘主来调侃张翰。	Jin Ling doesn't like others using "pond owner" to ridicule Zhang Han.	蓝曦臣认为网络上的塘主争议很有意思。	Lan Xichen finds the online controversy over "pond owner" very interesting.
好单纯好不做作	<Expression> So innocent, so unpretentious. This Internet meme was made popular by vlogger @谷阿莫 in his synopses of movies and TV series. This term is usually used to explain the reason why the male lead fell in love with the female lead.	魏无羡觉得女主角好单纯好不做作。	Wei Wuxian thinks the female lead is so innocent and unpretentious.	金凌不明白为什么男主角会喜欢女主角，觉得她好单纯好不做作。	Jin Ling doesn't understand why the male lead would like the female lead, thinking she is so innocent and unpretentious.	蓝曦臣喜欢看@谷阿莫的影评，觉得他说的好单纯好不做作很有道理。	Lan Xichen likes to watch @Gu Amo's movie reviews and thinks his explanation of "so innocent, so unpretentious" makes sense.
霸道总裁	/handsome high-powered businessman (a type of character in an eponymous genre of romantic fiction who typically has a soft spot for a girl of lower social status)/	魏无羡觉得霸道总裁这种角色很有趣。	Wei Wuxian finds the character of a handsome high-powered businessman very interesting.	金凌喜欢看言情小说，特别喜欢霸道总裁这种角色。	Jin Ling likes to read romance novels, especially the character of a handsome high-powered businessman.	蓝曦臣觉得霸道总裁这种角色有点刻板。	Lan Xichen thinks the character of a handsome high-powered businessman is a bit stereotypical.

居老师	n. Teacher Ju. This Internet slang term is a nickname for Chinese actor Zhu Yilong who is most well-known for his role in the popular web series Guardian. 居 [jū] is the pronunciation of his surname 朱 [zhū] Zhu in the Wuhan dialect, his hometown dialect.	居老师在《镇魂》中的表演令人印象深刻。	Teacher Ju's performance in "Guardian" left a deep impression.	居老师的粉丝们对他的新剧期待很高。	Fans of Teacher Ju have high expectations for his new drama.	居老师的幽默风趣深受粉丝喜爱。	Teacher Ju's humor and wit are deeply loved by fans.
脑斧	n. Brain+ax. Tiger. This Internet slang term mimics the pronunciation of 老虎 [lǎo hǔ] “tiger” with accents that do not differentiate between “h” and “f” in Pinyin.	他的外号是“脑斧”，听起来很有意思。	His nickname is "Brain+ax," which sounds very interesting.	在网上，很多粉丝都称他为“脑斧”。	Many fans online refer to him as "Brain+ax."	“脑斧”这个绰号真是太有创意了。	The nickname "Brain+ax" is really creative.
上辈子拯救了银河系	Rescued the Milky Way in one’s previous life. This Internet slang phrase is used to express your envy or jealousy toward the people who got something you desire. You joke that their good luck implies good karma.	他得到了那份工作，我上辈子拯救了银河系吗？	He got that job, did I rescue the Milky Way in my previous life?	她居然中了大奖，我上辈子拯救了银河系吗？	She actually won the grand prize, did I rescue the Milky Way in my previous life?	他怎么能这么幸运？我上辈子拯救了银河系吗？	How can he be so lucky? Did I rescue the Milky Way in my previous life?
这是。。。被黑得最惨的一次	<Expression> This is the time when… was roasted/humiliated most seriously. This expression is often used humorously to refer to an often unexpected embarrassing situation where someone or an organization is caught in, especially when they are unintentionally put down.	这是他被黑得最惨的一次，真是让人忍俊不禁。	This is the time when he was roasted most seriously, it's really hard not to laugh.	这是我们公司被黑得最惨的一次，真是让人哭笑不得。	This is the time when our company was humiliated most seriously, it's really laughable and exasperating.	这是他被黑得最惨的一次，大家都忍不住笑了出来。	This is the time when he was roasted most seriously, everyone couldn't help but laugh.
抖机灵	<Expression> Shake+cleverness. Make a wisecrack. This expression is used slightly negatively to describe people who quip to show off how witty they are.	他总是喜欢在会议上抖机灵，有点让人受不了。	He always likes to make wisecracks at meetings, it's a bit unbearable.	别老抖机灵了，有时候认真一点更重要。	Stop showing off how witty you are, sometimes being serious is more important.	她抖机灵的时候，总能逗得大家哈哈大笑。	When she makes wisecracks, she always manages to make everyone laugh.

苏 (=酥)	adj. (Of a person’s limbs) weak, soft	蓝忘机的琴声如此悠扬，听了让人感到全身都苏了。	Lan Wangji's qin playing is so melodious, listening to it makes one feel relaxed all over.	魏无羡的微笑让人心头一松，仿佛全身都苏了。	Wei Wuxian's smile makes people feel at ease, as if their whole body has softened.	金凌看到舅舅送给他的小狗，眼睛里闪着苏的光芒。	Jin Ling's eyes lit up with a soft glow when he saw the puppy his uncle gave him.
反射弧过长	<Expression> The reflex arc is too long	蓝曦臣发现问题的速度总是那么快，他的反射弧从来都不会过长。	Lan Xichen always discovers problems so quickly; his reflex arc is never too long.	魏无羡对于解决难题总是反应迅速，从不会有反射弧过长的情况。	Wei Wuxian always reacts quickly to solve difficult problems; there is never a situation of a too long reflex arc.	江澄虽然性情急躁，但是对于发现问题的速度却从不会有反射弧过长的情况。	Although Jiang Cheng has a hot temper, he never has a too long reflex arc when it comes to discovering problems.
饭随爱豆	<Expression> The fans and their idols share similar qualities	蓝忘机的音乐品味与他的粉丝们如此相似，可以说是饭随爱豆。	Lan Wangji's music taste is so similar to that of his fans; it can be said that the fans and their idol share similar qualities.	魏无羡的幽默风趣与粉丝们如此相似，可以说是饭随爱豆。	Wei Wuxian's humor and wit are so similar to that of his fans; it can be said that the fans and their idol share similar qualities.	金凌的性格与他的粉丝们如此相似，可以说是饭随爱豆。	Jin Ling's personality is so similar to that of his fans; it can be said that the fans and their idol share similar qualities.
宇宙观	/world view/	蓝曦臣的宇宙观是如此宽广，深不可测。	Lan Xichen's world view is so broad and profound.	魏无羡的宇宙观总是充满着奇思妙想，让人叹为观止。	Wei Wuxian's world view is always full of fantastic ideas, which is truly amazing.	江澄的宇宙观总是充满正义感，对于善恶的判断总是一针见血。	Jiang Cheng's world view is always full of a sense of justice, and his judgment of good and evil is always incisive.
小确丧	n. Little+definite+frustration	温情的微笑掩饰不住他内心的小确丧。	The warm smile cannot conceal the little definite frustration in his heart.	魏无羡的玩世不恭只是他内心小确丧的一种表现。	Wei Wuxian's carefree attitude is just a manifestation of his little definite frustration in his heart.	金凌的坚强外表下隐藏着内心的小确丧。	Beneath Jin Ling's strong exterior lies the little definite frustration in his heart.

扶我上墙	<Expression> Help me get onto the wall. Help me become more visible in this online discussion by liking my post.	魏无羡在论坛上发了一篇帖子，请求粉丝们扶他上墙。	Wei Wuxian posted on the forum, asking his fans to help him get more visibility.	蓝忘机的照片被粉丝们扶上墙了，引起了热烈的讨论。	Lan Wangji's photo was promoted by fans to get more visibility, sparking heated discussions.	金凌请求大家扶他上墙，希望能够得到更多的关注。	Jin Ling asked everyone to help him get onto the wall, hoping to get more attention.
开封菜	n. The Kaifeng cuisine. This Internet slang term is a humorous moniker for KFC, because they share the acronym.	魏无羡和江澄约好一起吃开封菜，结果却去了KFC。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng agreed to eat Kaifeng cuisine together, but ended up going to KFC.	金凌问蓝曦臣想吃开封菜还是KFC，两人纠结了半天。	Jin Ling asked Lan Xichen whether he wanted to eat Kaifeng cuisine or KFC, and the two of them were indecisive for a long time.	蓝忘机不喜欢吃快餐，更喜欢品尝正宗的开封菜。	Lan Wangji doesn't like fast food and prefers to taste authentic Kaifeng cuisine.
谢耳朵	n. Xie+ear. Xie Ear. This Internet slang term combines the Chinese last name Xie and the word ear. It is an affectionate nickname for American actor Jim Parsons and his role Sheldon Lee Cooper in The Big Bang Theory.	魏无羡和蓝忘机在一起看《生活大爆炸》，讨论谢耳朵的角色。	Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji watched "The Big Bang Theory" together and discussed Xie Ear's character.	金凌很喜欢谢耳朵，经常模仿他的经典台词。	Jin Ling really likes Xie Ear and often imitates his classic lines.	蓝曦臣觉得谢耳朵在《生活大爆炸》里的表演非常出色。	Lan Xichen thinks Xie Ear's performance in "The Big Bang Theory" is excellent.
这货	n. This dude, often used in casual conversation among Chinese young people.	魏无羡看着蓝忘机，心想：“这货怎么又在修剑？”	Wei Wuxian looked at Lan Wangji and thought, "Why is this dude practicing swordsmanship again?"	金凌对着镜子整理衣服，自言自语：“这货真是越来越帅了。”	Jin Ling tidied his clothes in front of the mirror and muttered to himself, "This dude is getting more and more handsome."	蓝曦臣看着魏无羡，感慨地说：“这货，又惹祸了。”	Lan Xichen looked at Wei Wuxian and sighed, "This dude has caused trouble again."
